				var instance = this;

						searchExp: '\\.js$'
					};
				}

				return filterConfig;
			},

				return '/o/frontend-js-web';
			},

				return '/html/portlet';
			},

				return '?browserId=other&minifierType=&languageId=en_GB&t=1753850629520';
			}
		};

        <script>
            $(document).ready(function() {
                $('div.cpm-text-description p').each(function () {
                    replaceConsentHtmlContent(this);
                });

                $('span.text-truncate-container p').each(function () {
                    replaceConsentHtmlContent(this);
                });

                $('#textLegalContent .consentText p').each(function() {
                    replaceConsentHtmlContent(this);
                });

                $('#agreement.legalText p').each(function() {
                    replaceConsentHtmlContent(this);
                });
            });

            function replaceConsentHtmlContent(thisObj) {
                let htmlContent = {};
                $(thisObj).children().each(function (index) {
                    let param = "anchor"+index
                    $(this).html(parseHtmlContent($(this).html()))
                    htmlContent[param] = $(this)
                    $(this).replaceWith( param);
                })
                let inputContent = $(thisObj).html();
                let textContent = parseHtmlContent(inputContent);


                $(thisObj).html(textContent);
                inputContent = $(thisObj).html();
                $.each(htmlContent, function (key, data) {
                    inputContent =inputContent.replace(key , data[0].outerHTML);
                });
                $(thisObj).html(inputContent);
            }

            function parseHtmlContent(input) {
                let doc = new DOMParser().parseFromString(input, "text/html");
                return doc.documentElement.textContent;
            }
        </script>

        function getCookiePref(cookieName) {
          let cookie = {};
          document.cookie.split(';').forEach(function(el) {
            let [key,value] = el.split('=');
            cookie[key.trim()] = value;
          })
          return cookie[cookieName];
        }

    <script>
        window.addEventListener("load", function() {
            let isConsentProvided = false;
            if(typeof truste !== "undefined"){
                const TRUST_FUNCTIONAL = 2;
                let result = truste.cma.callApi("getConsentDecision", window.location.host);
                if (result.consentDecision >= TRUST_FUNCTIONAL) {
                    isConsentProvided = true;
                    if(window.location.href.includes('#')){
                        var scrollDivId= window.location.href.split("#")[1];
                        $('html, body').animate({
                            scrollTop: $("#"+scrollDivId).offset().top
                        }, 2000);
                    }
                }
            }
            if (document.referrer && !document.referrer.includes(".hays.")) {
                localStorage.setItem("hays-referrer-ext", document.referrer);
            }
            if (!isConsentProvided) {
                window['ac_client_disable_tracking'] = true;
            }
        });

        //handling the Trust Arc...
        window.addEventListener("message", function(event){
            let eventDataJson  = null;
            try {
                eventDataJson = JSON.parse(event.data);
            } catch(exp) {

            }

            if (eventDataJson && eventDataJson.source === 'preference_manager'
                && eventDataJson.message === 'submit_preferences') {
                window.location.reload();
            }


        });
    </script>

<script>

    var parentHeight = 0;
    $(".nav-list__item").mouseenter(function () {
        if($(this).hasClass('nav-list__item_child')) {
            var lengthOfChild =  $(this).children().length;
            if (lengthOfChild > 1) {
                var childHeight =  $(this).children('div.container-grid-third').children('ul.nav-list__third').height();
                childHeight =  1.1 * childHeight;
                if(parentHeight == 0) {
                    parentHeight = $(this).parents('ul.nav-list__first').parent('.container-grid-first').height();
                }
                var height = Math.max(childHeight, parentHeight);
                $(this).parents('ul.nav-list__first').parent('.container-grid-first').height(height);
            }else {
                if (parentHeight != 0) {
                    $(this).parents('ul.nav-list__first').parent('.container-grid-first').height(parentHeight);
                    parentHeight = 0;
                }

            }
        }

    })


    $("#accessibility").click(function () {
        $("#eyeAble_columID").css("display", "block");
    });

</script>

            <script type="text/javascript">
                // Generate the searchHistory module
                $(function () {
                    $('#searchbarForm').searchHistory({
                        'sendWhenSelect': true,
                        'maxShowNum': 5,
                        'actionByCall': true,
                        'lang': "en_GB"
                    });

                    $("#what").click(function (e) {
                        if ($("#what").val().length > 0) {
                            $('#searchbarForm').searchHistory('close');
                        } else {
                            $('#searchbarForm').searchHistory('open');
                        }
                    });

                    $("#what").keyup(function (e) {
                        if ($("#what").val().length > 0) {
                            $('#searchbarForm').searchHistory('close');
                        } else {
                            $('#searchbarForm').searchHistory('open');
                        }
                    });

                });

            </script>

</ul>
	
</nav>

	
	
					
				
			
		
	
	


	</div>

	</div>
</section>

}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-h-dropzone-990px lfr-layout-structure-item-462d5d1a-959a-c972-fbfd-7c0878ebe784 " style=""><div id="fragment-599b03e3-3df4-c18d-043b-a227df378d61"> <div class="fragment_1">  <div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-heading lfr-layout-structure-item-362b70f2-1a32-0470-604d-0d326f4bec11 " style=""><div id="fragment-d8a59bc0-c903-22c1-ba12-91ceeb45c48e"> <h2 class="component-heading mb-0 text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="text">The controller profession: more than just a number cruncher</h2></div><style>.fragment-heading-text-colored a {
	color: inherit;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-824fb23c-47da-52e9-2692-857556d1e337 " style=""><div id="fragment-56601f1e-f0b4-ca3e-f96d-c0ce5597ba14"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-1e328256-28d4-66ee-f794-ba19050307c8 " style=""><div id="fragment-7b773898-6503-f605-261f-913cd0cd5c46"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">What exactly do controllers do? To put it simply, controllers keep an eye on the company's current internal figures at all times. They are responsible for evaluating them and advising the management on the right strategic and operational decisions within the company.</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-b6431900-9d83-0416-81ef-c51dd7773c52 " style=""><div id="fragment-e38ba787-0a2c-62bc-61c7-3d9dc28c86a8"> <div class="py-3"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-75be1c2e-2734-2174-4d72-c71e2749328a lfr-layout-structure-item-row " style=""><div class="row align-items-lg-start align-items-sm-start align-items-start align-items-md-start flex-lg-row flex-sm-row flex-row flex-md-row"><div class="col col-lg-8 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-8"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-537b587d-f105-31ab-4199-ef5ed6e4b713 " style=""><div id="fragment-70477b8d-0361-e624-d045-2b00e6aaecbf"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><h2>CONTENT</h2>
<a href="#Aufgaben" rel="noopener noreferrer">►</a><a href="#tasks" rel="noopener noreferrer">&nbsp;Tasks</a><br />
<a href="#gehalt" rel="noopener noreferrer">►&nbsp;</a><a href="#salary" rel="noopener noreferrer">Salary</a><br />
<a href="#ausbildung-skills" rel="noopener noreferrer">►&nbsp;</a><a href="#training-skills" rel="noopener noreferrer">Training/Skills</a></div></div></div></div><div class="col col-lg-4 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-4"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-image lfr-layout-structure-item-3d4d15ff-0d16-638f-e088-e4a54c6869fc " style=""><div id="fragment-8392c39b-5589-b0b3-0393-33606b8b7446"> <div class="component-image overflow-hidden">
	<picture data-fileentryid="3126882373"><source media="(max-width:225px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3126882373/1000px-till-1280px-width/MicrosoftTeams-image+%2810%29.png?t=1668696978683" /><source media="(max-width:225px) and (min-width:225px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3126882373/480px-width/MicrosoftTeams-image+%2810%29.png?t=1668696978683" /><source media="(max-width:225px) and (min-width:225px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3126882373/980px-width/MicrosoftTeams-image+%2810%29.png?t=1668696978683" /><source media="(max-width:225px) and (min-width:225px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3126882373/high-resolution/MicrosoftTeams-image+%2810%29.png?t=1668696978683" /><source media="(max-width:225px) and (min-width:225px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3126882373/Preview-1000x0/MicrosoftTeams-image+%2810%29.png?t=1668696978683" /><source media="(max-width:225px) and (min-width:225px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3126882373/thumbnail-300x300/MicrosoftTeams-image+%2810%29.png?t=1668696978683" /><img alt="" class="w-0" data-lfr-editable-id="image-square" data-lfr-editable-type="image" src="/documents/10695/0/MicrosoftTeams-image%2B%2810%29.png/b8ced25f-0a1f-3d94-e880-a5f17450ce39?version=1.0&amp;t=1668696978683" data-fileentryid="3126882373" loading="lazy" /></picture>
</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-208076f5-f15b-e159-9f6c-8200b35bbe95 " style=""><div id="fragment-18b5673b-1662-5557-ecd1-0551cb5ef94c"> <div class="py-3"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-d2b405d9-cf5b-4e9d-e547-ea044039abcd " style=""><div id="fragment-d614bfd5-4417-3de2-8702-22765aed3aab"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><h3>The controller at a glance</h3>
Checking figures is therefore definitely part of the job, but controllers are more like number crunchers. In addition to preparing evaluations and reports, they plan and manage processes and services with the aim of ensuring the company's profitability. Controlling is therefore a management task.<br />
<br />
In addition to analytical skills, the role of Controller (m/f/d) requires above all open and friendly interaction with colleagues. This is because Controlling works very closely with IT, business analysts and decision-makers from all areas of the company. Only through this overarching cooperation can controlling specialists recognize new potential for their own company and weigh up costs and risks.<br />
<br />
Controllers have a varied and responsible profession, as their work contributes significantly to the current and future development of the company and thus ensures the competitiveness of companies.<br />
<br />
&nbsp;</div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-5d337b1f-3415-3843-a72e-950530070cb3 " style=""><div id="fragment-d5eb6a40-92e3-119e-d605-7aef8f5f125c"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-heading lfr-layout-structure-item-181a3166-1d98-7222-5a42-097f9ff8fa21 " style=""><div id="fragment-b8e9f903-ab76-3541-74c2-b2331444af5f"> <h3 class="component-heading mb-0 text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="text">Key Facts</h3></div><style>.fragment-heading-text-colored a {
	color: inherit;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-8cae9f63-a20a-d2a5-5ae7-6469e7e292f4 " style=""><div id="fragment-4c323cf6-1d82-3036-e474-497f7d9a407c"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-f833ae9c-cd87-212f-7318-0c23bc8214f7 lfr-layout-structure-item-row " style=""><div class="row align-items-lg-start align-items-sm-start align-items-start align-items-md-start flex-lg-row flex-sm-row flex-row flex-md-row"><div class="col col-lg-8 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-8"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-4ace7300-11df-30d3-d450-2d94a3b865ae " style=""><div id="fragment-898c540e-084f-34fd-1f4f-d1daff4f879e"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><h4>Role of the controller</h4>
Financial expert who plans, analyzes and optimizes business processes<br />
&nbsp;
<h4>Education</h4>
Studies or training in the commercial sector plus further training as a controller<br />
&nbsp;
<h4>Further training</h4>

<p>Specializations in various areas of controlling</p>

<h4>Salary</h4>
50,000 to 70,000 euros on average, up to 100,000 euros possible<br />
&nbsp;
<h4>Hard &amp; Soft Skills</h4>
► Training and experience in controlling and accounting<br />
► Analytical and planning skills<br />
► Knowledge of relevant IT applications and software<br />
► Knowledge of English<br />
► Ability to work under pressure, flexibility, assertiveness<br />
&nbsp;</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div></div><div class="col col-lg-4 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-4"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-657c3f15-a96b-3bb6-d129-4ef96348e952 " style=""><div id="fragment-5df33146-25a0-c223-7b75-22b758361716"> <div class="py-5"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-bb80bf41-ac4a-3bb7-b5f1-6a8a62e94fa0 " style=""><div id="fragment-d03f79de-67c2-8a98-6c17-d1356066610d"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-image lfr-layout-structure-item-ba595a2a-7cc6-584b-1727-f428f2606dbf " style=""><div id="fragment-365de6a7-77fc-58ba-a0ea-06812ffbf971"> <div class="component-image overflow-hidden">

}</style></div></div> 
 </div>
</div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-h-dropzone-990px lfr-layout-structure-item-b170aff5-04a9-b4c4-1cff-aee7835bedc0 " style=""><div id="fragment-155f842a-9577-6b99-3d36-d3aeff4bc68a"> <div class="fragment_1">  <div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-e5815866-72d0-52d3-ed96-16aec330b65d " style=""><div id="fragment-4395397b-d72a-377f-a6a7-833bb73f4bf1"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-a5d60714-b343-edf9-f009-819fabd9724d " style=""><div id="fragment-b546b0b1-8aa9-9de0-a493-ff6ea6fcf37e"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-html lfr-layout-structure-item-20993778-5c8a-c5e7-5f88-5c4b83a9c839 " style=""><div id="fragment-b451b7f4-53f4-b32f-ddb5-2d1ab3562e1b"> <div class="component-html" data-lfr-editable-id="element-html" data-lfr-editable-type="html"><h2 id="tasks">Controller tasks: <strong>What activities are part of a controller's everyday life?
</strong></h2>
</div></div><style>.component-html img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-f37a407a-1470-489e-a6a3-964662b740fa " style=""><div id="fragment-25630e5b-9468-013a-5403-32b536513f3a"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-57a516b3-9c27-5a91-922a-01d17147ce53 " style=""><div id="fragment-42044e0a-6cd3-dd8f-92a8-6241f4803dc2"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">As an area of a company's accounting system, namely internal accounting, controlling plans, directs and manages company processes. The aim of controlling is to keep a company on the road to success or to get it there. Always with the aim of maximizing profits. And this happens on an ongoing basis and not just at the end of a financial year. The continuous review of business figures enables controllers to recommend short-term measures in order to intervene to correct unfavorable company developments.<br />
<br />
In contrast, a company's external accounting, and with it its financial accounting, records figures for information to third parties, such as the tax office or shareholders. These are figures from the past that are analyzed in order to draw up a balance sheet at the end of an observation period and to disclose whether controlling has worked successfully.<br />
<br />
Controlling managers are therefore responsible for planning, controlling and monitoring processes and play a key role in the company's development. The following tasks are part of the day-to-day work of a controller (m/f/d):</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-ecb30577-4c7e-74da-3fce-be9ec9b64b2a lfr-layout-structure-item-row " style=""><div class="row align-items-lg-start align-items-sm-start align-items-start align-items-md-start flex-lg-row flex-sm-row flex-row flex-md-row"><div class="col col-lg-7 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-7"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-969cedeb-38b7-d04d-305d-fe9c97031b3e " style=""><div id="fragment-5f80119c-3c69-b894-7cce-e59582e8d8b5"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><br />
► Determination and control of processes in the company<br />
► Analysis and optimization of processes<br />
► Process and weak point analysis and continuous optimization<br />
► Target/actual comparisons<br />
► Budget planning and sales forecasts<br />
► Planning and implementation of strategies<br />
► Preparation and transmission of figures to management</div></div></div></div><div class="col col-lg-5 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-5"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-2ca26460-861b-9f39-1eba-121c49fcba92 " style=""><div id="fragment-3e47af5f-dc08-02b8-297a-e58d413ecd63"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-image lfr-layout-structure-item-58dc3c83-4b8d-53cf-47c9-028d916eca65 " style=""><div id="fragment-b455acaf-2619-2daf-91cb-d545e6674cca"> <div class="component-image overflow-hidden">
	<picture data-fileentryid="3437607974"><source media="(max-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3437607974/1000px-till-1280px-width/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png?t=1688536579794" /><source media="(max-width:300px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3437607974/480px-width/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png?t=1688536579794" /><source media="(max-width:300px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3437607974/980px-width/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png?t=1688536579794" /><source media="(max-width:300px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3437607974/high-resolution/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png?t=1688536579794" /><source media="(max-width:300px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3437607974/Preview-1000x0/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png?t=1688536579794" /><source media="(max-width:300px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3437607974/thumbnail-300x300/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png?t=1688536579794" /><img alt="" class="w-100" data-lfr-editable-id="image-square" data-lfr-editable-type="image" src="/documents/10695/0/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png/45ace8e2-634c-dd96-bd7d-70de9539bf89?version=1.0&amp;t=1688536579794" data-fileentryid="3437607974" loading="lazy" /></picture>
</div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-image lfr-layout-structure-item-aed53607-9fe8-eeda-4d02-50764570eba7 " style=""><div id="fragment-a8b8d7e6-35ab-c582-a53c-ad5f2b14fcb9"> <div class="component-image overflow-hidden">
	<picture data-fileentryid="3437607974"><source media="(max-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3437607974/1000px-till-1280px-width/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png?t=1688536579794" /><source media="(max-width:300px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3437607974/480px-width/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png?t=1688536579794" /><source media="(max-width:300px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3437607974/980px-width/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png?t=1688536579794" /><source media="(max-width:300px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3437607974/high-resolution/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png?t=1688536579794" /><source media="(max-width:300px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3437607974/Preview-1000x0/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png?t=1688536579794" /><source media="(max-width:300px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3437607974/thumbnail-300x300/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png?t=1688536579794" /><img alt="" class="w-100" data-lfr-editable-id="image-square" data-lfr-editable-type="image" src="/documents/10695/0/HW_Rubriken_Dreiecke.png/45ace8e2-634c-dd96-bd7d-70de9539bf89?version=1.0&amp;t=1688536579794" data-fileentryid="3437607974" loading="lazy" /></picture>
</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-5a6c4cfe-c2e0-7d75-3bc5-6e371ab13ee1 " style=""><div id="fragment-437a89e4-6e3d-7c1a-e1f3-f0ed49a47173"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-a100ae99-d106-93f4-fed3-2c680dcc79bd " style=""><div id="fragment-9e2218e2-43fc-d2f7-5aa5-725546de4b6f"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">Depending on their area of responsibility, controllers in operational controlling are responsible for budget management, i.e. the economic efficiency and profitability of the company. In strategic controlling, on the other hand, they look for new potential for the company and weigh up costs and risks.<br />
But it is not only the responsibilities that differ in controlling. Depending on the area of tasks and responsibilities, companies and organizations fill the respective position with controllers - according to their qualifications and previous experience:</div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-26505b90-8a1b-df05-a98e-c19d00dfde1b " style=""><div id="fragment-85fcea97-dd2c-6a60-5889-42de385be5b5"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-com-liferay-fragment-internal-renderer-contentobjectfragmentrenderer lfr-layout-structure-item-779ec465-c6df-ba3b-d347-2e892e32ac8f " style="">

            $(this).css('display', 'none');

    if (handlerAttached == false) {
        $( "div.fold-content-template div.fold-headline h3" ).click(function() {
                    var contentTemplateDiv = $(this).parentsUntil("div.fold-content-template").parent();
                    var contentDiv = contentTemplateDiv.find('.fold-content');
                    var contentTeaser = contentTemplateDiv.find('.fold-content-teaser');
                    var aFoldLinkOpen = contentTemplateDiv.find('a.fold-link-open');
                    var aFoldLinkClose = contentTemplateDiv.find('a.fold-link-close');
                    if (contentDiv.css('display') == 'none') {
                    aFoldLinkOpen.css('display', 'none');
                    aFoldLinkClose.css('display', 'inline-block');
                    contentDiv.fadeIn('fast');
                    contentTeaser.toggle();
                    } else {
                    aFoldLinkOpen.css('display', 'inline-block');
                    aFoldLinkClose.css('display', 'none');
                    contentDiv.fadeOut('fast');
                    contentTeaser.toggle();
                    }
                });
                handlerAttached = true;
                }
    });
</script>

</div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-5a9d9f1a-8c0d-211a-4088-ab3dc4ad85cd " style=""><div id="fragment-1fc7e6f4-b587-3a3d-81d8-946fdd1040f3"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-40d18a2f-7fc0-0445-1fac-96676ccd1579 " style=""><div id="fragment-5e4aba75-a07e-5389-7bc2-41d07bd16db3"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-html lfr-layout-structure-item-3775c1a3-58e9-dae7-8f77-7f730b31fe4f " style=""><div id="fragment-a4429550-5600-902f-670c-7b83a9f597cf"> <div class="component-html" data-lfr-editable-id="element-html" data-lfr-editable-type="html">
	<h2 id="salary">What does a controller earn?</h2>
</div></div><style>.component-html img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-df3c1def-505b-e9d5-17e2-5fe9a3bff6d6 " style=""><div id="fragment-a7e411b7-ba14-5e7d-79df-6f3ae0f51231"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-heading lfr-layout-structure-item-9e46211b-2cfa-01c7-f8ae-31d81941b8cb " style=""><div id="fragment-ea223bae-e12b-20a3-cc57-6250ed0e3b91"> <h3 class="component-heading mb-0 text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="text">Junior controller salary: What is the starting salary for a controller?</h3></div><style>.fragment-heading-text-colored a {
	color: inherit;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-5e1bf293-9bb4-eb26-0c01-410c3fa72ed5 " style=""><div id="fragment-d15c2c97-502d-cdd6-9ba2-277a0d7dff0e"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-5cdf7bfc-3bea-02a4-baba-441fb2ace5a3 " style=""><div id="fragment-7f0bd811-d757-0012-fbd4-7f947f624c80"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">Controlling is a management task and the position of controlling manager is also anchored at this level. The great responsibility of controllers is also reflected in their salaries. Junior controllers (m/f/d) can expect a starting salary of around 45,000 euros gross per year.</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-cdb993ff-4990-97f6-d69e-45f704c2bb72 " style=""><div id="fragment-e3b0cd8e-839a-df67-9df5-1f51b96948e0"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-heading lfr-layout-structure-item-a95c941a-8694-db8a-b439-146fc7d169d5 " style=""><div id="fragment-24541c33-1913-dc91-6e5e-ba7da3d8347c"> <h3 class="component-heading mb-0 text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="text">Senior Controller salary: How much do you earn with experience?</h3></div><style>.fragment-heading-text-colored a {
	color: inherit;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-c833ef0b-7f77-de6f-e794-e13a0ee111c2 " style=""><div id="fragment-ae59fb23-5dda-7b8a-e16c-6f72ba3b795c"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-d5b54ff1-2a43-d1be-40af-c847d2de69e9 " style=""><div id="fragment-b8d39a4d-6a2c-3157-fa43-ff627222edd5"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">As professional experience and responsibility increase, the contribution of this position to the company's success becomes more and more apparent. This is also reflected in the salary. As a senior controlling manager, people in this role can expect a significantly higher salary. Depending on the size of the company and their own area of responsibility, annual salaries of between 60,000 and 115,000 euros gross are the order of the day. Above all, controllers with a degree in business administration and a specialized Master's degree are sought-after specialists in controlling.</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-01ea0244-0fd5-85d8-331d-699ef314151a " style=""><div id="fragment-eecbfe7a-bb15-8769-f0f3-4bf7cb21c47b"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-heading lfr-layout-structure-item-176856ac-d12b-4cc0-3898-dc48c5934d73 " style=""><div id="fragment-d7e22f5f-1314-17df-1af5-e037e65b0e8d"> <h3 class="component-heading mb-0 text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="text">Can controllers specialize?</h3></div><style>.fragment-heading-text-colored a {
	color: inherit;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-fd4e33a9-0c39-b5f4-bf4a-faaf7bfcc6ae " style=""><div id="fragment-75595466-0b68-dd10-eb94-a2360207c298"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-9a40cb62-256e-fe01-37b8-01d95ed8c68f " style=""><div id="fragment-d94477d8-e792-91b4-312b-d88212b2db5b"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">In large companies, individual divisions or departments may have their own controlling department. Accordingly, experts in controlling can also specialize in the following areas:<br />
<br />
► Sales controlling<br />
► Logistics controlling<br />
► Investment controlling<br />
► Marketing logistics<br />
► Production controlling</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-5e3fcd6c-f0c3-09b3-da22-fce40e0750a1 " style=""><div id="fragment-cfda4368-d515-4f82-d1d3-1a1d2ac7bb07"> <div class="py-3"></div></div></div></div> 
 </div>
</div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-h-dropzone-990px lfr-layout-structure-item-4844793b-313c-0c9a-e903-45190fa23536 " style=""><div id="fragment-f8a6eeab-91a2-628c-40a2-f5a8c1b671a7"> <div class="fragment_1">  <div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-heading lfr-layout-structure-item-c9b23ecb-7885-d0b9-3950-72326992c8e0 " style=""><div id="fragment-3137ee20-725e-305b-a9f5-43dc104d953f"> <h3 class="component-heading mb-0 text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="text">What hard and soft skills should controllers have?</h3></div><style>.fragment-heading-text-colored a {
	color: inherit;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-432b01b4-f767-e5f8-76cd-8f14586af625 " style=""><div id="fragment-209d1f85-3bac-f5fa-07c8-82faca723250"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-da1ec0ee-76af-4118-65f5-1d1a11129979 " style=""><div id="fragment-dc87da6d-6a88-1ef6-0420-da4e6156a775"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">In addition to analytical thinking and planning skills, controllers should have a high degree of persuasiveness and assertiveness. They are often the ones who have to explain the collected company figures and data in presentations and justify their recommendations. An eye for the essentials and a good command of English are a must for specialists in controlling in their role as the right hand of the company management.</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-7cf4fa7e-bafc-9dc4-c277-90d0007ddb52 lfr-layout-structure-item-row " style=""><div class="row align-items-lg-start align-items-sm-start align-items-start align-items-md-start flex-lg-row flex-sm-row flex-row flex-md-row"><div class="col col-lg-6 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-6"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-21be9bf7-042b-f733-4b46-7bd031201f91 " style=""><div id="fragment-65b40689-1961-98d0-74ee-f79f62cf4b59"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">The following hard and soft skills characterize controllers:<br />
<br />
► Training and experience in controlling and accounting<br />
► Analytical and planning skills<br />
► Knowledge of relevant IT applications and software<br />
► Knowledge of English<br />
► Ability to work under pressure, flexibility, assertiveness<br />
&nbsp;</div></div></div></div><div class="col col-lg-6 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-6"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-image lfr-layout-structure-item-7b1f55df-ea14-0186-f180-f20cd04a4d7c " style=""><div id="fragment-b782bf35-37cd-fc08-2434-f0d933b7304c"> <div class="component-image overflow-hidden">
	<picture data-fileentryid="3466969725"><source media="(max-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466969725/thumbnail-300x300/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png?t=1721294198459" /><source media="(max-width:480px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466969725/480px-width/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png?t=1721294198459" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:480px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466969725/1000px-till-1280px-width/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png?t=1721294198459" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466969725/980px-width/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png?t=1721294198459" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466969725/high-resolution/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png?t=1721294198459" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466969725/Preview-1000x0/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png?t=1721294198459" /><img alt="" class="w-100" data-lfr-editable-id="image-square" data-lfr-editable-type="image" src="/documents/10192/3466712379/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png/3c3b99e0-75bc-024f-d247-fe8c5844b9a2?version=2.0&amp;t=1721294198459" data-fileentryid="3466969725" loading="lazy" /></picture>
</div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-image lfr-layout-structure-item-9f998549-7e34-819f-67c8-3769b96e1876 " style=""><div id="fragment-01017443-5e45-17e8-5c85-cab9855d448d"> <div class="component-image overflow-hidden">
	<picture data-fileentryid="3466969725"><source media="(max-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466969725/thumbnail-300x300/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png?t=1721294198459" /><source media="(max-width:480px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466969725/480px-width/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png?t=1721294198459" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:480px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466969725/1000px-till-1280px-width/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png?t=1721294198459" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466969725/980px-width/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png?t=1721294198459" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466969725/high-resolution/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png?t=1721294198459" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466969725/Preview-1000x0/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png?t=1721294198459" /><img alt="" class="w-100" data-lfr-editable-id="image-square" data-lfr-editable-type="image" src="/documents/10192/3466712379/Isometric+Illustrations_Positive+Thinking.png/3c3b99e0-75bc-024f-d247-fe8c5844b9a2?version=2.0&amp;t=1721294198459" data-fileentryid="3466969725" loading="lazy" /></picture>
</div></div></div></div></div></div></div> 
 </div>
</div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-ebb93250-82e1-5469-a69f-0be5f577723f " style=""><div id="fragment-d4412b4c-7900-57e8-e609-5919088fecc4"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-f5bd3c58-646d-2d3b-c731-ba0ed8f0689d " style=""><div id="fragment-4ad7bd4b-0b96-40b5-afe0-1b37f3f58bf1"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-h-dropzone-990px lfr-layout-structure-item-4a78399b-5268-5c70-2ace-42e0515c8040 " style=""><div id="fragment-f50a6ace-92e0-b011-a52e-f47caf21c67f"> <div class="fragment_1">  <div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-html lfr-layout-structure-item-e4d8314c-fcb2-39a5-2305-20cbf0a59132 " style=""><div id="fragment-686283aa-be1d-4c92-3f62-acb3f8139763"> <div class="component-html" data-lfr-editable-id="element-html" data-lfr-editable-type="html"><h2 id="training-skills">Become a controller: <strong> What training should controllers have completed?</strong></h2>
</div></div><style>.component-html img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-a8345c2a-2472-9fee-243b-7a297744f079 " style=""><div id="fragment-ad243ef4-ba5c-7dcb-ac02-4d8165305cd9"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-8e755f18-96cf-2f3e-4902-f14fb61620e7 " style=""><div id="fragment-ef3bcc6e-812e-1bf0-dc93-9457d5de4264"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><div>As in many other professional fields, there is no one prescribed path to the goal in controlling. Anyone aspiring to a career in the role of a controller should acquire a sound knowledge of business administration and statistical skills. This can be achieved through a relevant course of study or training with subsequent further training.&nbsp;</div>
</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-a40501a0-771c-552e-01d7-1c1d78f8d440 " style=""><div id="fragment-9d552bca-5488-c0bb-398a-70f08743eefe"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-heading lfr-layout-structure-item-932cdc79-9e7e-f459-5966-f8b631db9069 " style=""><div id="fragment-823f848b-843d-c5e8-86be-a9d617e72d04"> <h3 class="component-heading mb-0 text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="text">The academic path - studying to become a controller</h3></div><style>.fragment-heading-text-colored a {
	color: inherit;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-1dfed6ec-8679-73f0-c741-2df25443651d " style=""><div id="fragment-e532bb59-791a-2dff-965a-09c7a27e7866"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-425cea6d-f78b-9e50-f245-43a2aebb1917 " style=""><div id="fragment-9b7e10ba-362a-46e4-7e8f-87ae6a2f7565"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">In addition to a degree in business administration with a focus on accounting or controlling, a degree course with a focus on mathematics or statistics is also an option. Many state and private universities offer full-time or part-time Bachelor's and Master's degree courses with different specializations. It is also possible to do a dual course of study in a company. The following courses are suitable for a career in controlling:<br />
&nbsp;</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-90cf197e-919c-fa04-efa9-c36f3c090b4a lfr-layout-structure-item-row " style=""><div class="row align-items-lg-start align-items-sm-start align-items-start align-items-md-start flex-lg-row flex-sm-row flex-row flex-md-row"><div class="col col-lg-6 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-6"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-38262a73-119f-9d76-7c6f-a797dbbc6cec " style=""><div id="fragment-a6bc2c6c-8028-8371-d839-7ea03cb1d8a3"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">► Banking and finance<br />
► European economy and corporate management<br />
► Finance, accounting &amp; taxation<br />
► Corporate management - Entrepreneurship<br />
► Business Administration (BWL)<br />
► International Management<br />
► General Management<br />
► Accounting &amp; Controlling</div></div></div></div><div class="col col-lg-6 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-6"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-image lfr-layout-structure-item-27810ffd-ca02-c471-5daf-c2a3f344888e " style=""><div id="fragment-e0440d1b-f0a7-36f2-8442-2c8dad38ede9"> <div class="component-image overflow-hidden">
	<picture data-fileentryid="3466970692"><source media="(max-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466970692/thumbnail-300x300/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png?t=1721294788337" /><source media="(max-width:480px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466970692/480px-width/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png?t=1721294788337" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:480px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466970692/1000px-till-1280px-width/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png?t=1721294788337" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466970692/980px-width/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png?t=1721294788337" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466970692/high-resolution/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png?t=1721294788337" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466970692/Preview-1000x0/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png?t=1721294788337" /><img alt="" class="w-100" data-lfr-editable-id="image-square" data-lfr-editable-type="image" src="/documents/10192/3466712379/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png/397c5670-db99-74e4-17bb-003e99ead32a?version=2.0&amp;t=1721294788337" data-fileentryid="3466970692" loading="lazy" /></picture>
</div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-image lfr-layout-structure-item-07dd3c13-b051-8f4a-05b4-f1c1f1f0588c " style=""><div id="fragment-a0a3d9d6-8443-42d3-55af-720be978c4dc"> <div class="component-image overflow-hidden">
	<picture data-fileentryid="3466970692"><source media="(max-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466970692/thumbnail-300x300/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png?t=1721294788337" /><source media="(max-width:480px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466970692/480px-width/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png?t=1721294788337" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:480px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466970692/1000px-till-1280px-width/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png?t=1721294788337" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466970692/980px-width/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png?t=1721294788337" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466970692/high-resolution/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png?t=1721294788337" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3466970692/Preview-1000x0/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png?t=1721294788337" /><img alt="" class="w-100" data-lfr-editable-id="image-square" data-lfr-editable-type="image" src="/documents/10192/3466712379/Isometric+Illustration_Books.png/397c5670-db99-74e4-17bb-003e99ead32a?version=2.0&amp;t=1721294788337" data-fileentryid="3466970692" loading="lazy" /></picture>
</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-8686f3a8-dd4a-65f9-a777-7dc9f9ef6687 " style=""><div id="fragment-384f01c2-8a05-7a1d-763f-b0034c3eb145"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-heading lfr-layout-structure-item-5530c7b1-ec45-828a-727d-9ca88ea66bc2 " style=""><div id="fragment-2b0dda4a-9759-409b-36f6-24bef0322f54"> <h3 class="component-heading mb-0 text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="text">How to become a Controller? Training &amp; Courses</h3></div><style>.fragment-heading-text-colored a {
	color: inherit;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-89548e64-ed83-2dff-f9a8-074201814609 " style=""><div id="fragment-649581b6-8053-feaa-15bc-21e911fa84bf"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-307a034b-e7e9-d9e4-6ffd-7dd12e8bf449 " style=""><div id="fragment-a883d0f4-71eb-0d8e-efa2-103ee754ba28"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">There are various ways in which you can become a controller. One option is to complete a commercial or administrative apprenticeship and then undertake further training to become a controller. This takes around 8 months on a part-time basis and provides you with the necessary knowledge in the areas of cost accounting, reporting, budgeting, information management and more1.<br />
<br />
Another option is to complete a business administration degree in which you can choose a specialization in controlling. This can be done at a university or university of applied sciences. A degree course offers you a broader theoretical basis and more opportunities to specialize in different areas of controlling.</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-c7039304-efc1-c799-55f2-3a38dd2d04c0 " style=""><div id="fragment-32f4ad31-3ff1-60df-ba73-65f1c8def9b8"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-heading lfr-layout-structure-item-8c94200f-5b44-a0be-53a4-d99d4ab2b2f8 " style=""><div id="fragment-f62013e4-fffa-aec6-cb70-a97bed395b0a"> <h3 class="component-heading mb-0 text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="text">Controller training</h3></div><style>.fragment-heading-text-colored a {
	color: inherit;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-8e0069df-18a7-c5c6-f3b2-7276082e272b " style=""><div id="fragment-7f1dae5a-65b1-b51e-9d70-0784c61d8b35"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-cccedec4-d55d-057c-b937-d11a8cff280b " style=""><div id="fragment-5ec68d98-85c4-b960-15f5-d10c9778a2b7"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">In order to develop as a controller and stay up to date, there are various options for controller training. These can vary depending on the objective, previous knowledge and time budget. The most popular forms of controller training include:<br />
&nbsp;
<ul>
	<li><strong>Certificate courses:</strong> These offer compact and practical training in specific controlling topics such as cost accounting, budgeting, reporting or risk management. The courses are offered by various providers such as the Chamber of Industry and Commerce, the Haufe Academy or the Controller Institute and conclude with a recognized certificate.&nbsp;</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

<ul>
	<li><strong>Distance learning:</strong> Distance learning allows you to design your controller training flexibly and individually. You can set your own pace and learning times and study from home. Distance learning can lead to an academic degree such as a Bachelor's or Master's in Controlling or to a part-time certificate such as Certified Controller.</li>
</ul>
&nbsp;

<ul>
	<li><strong>Seminars and workshops:</strong> These offer an intensive and interactive discussion of current controlling topics. They are aimed at controllers who want to deepen or refresh their knowledge or exchange ideas with other colleagues. Seminars and workshops are organized by various providers such as the Controller Association, Controller Magazin or the Controller Congress and usually last one to two days.</li>
</ul>
</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-b4374935-83c9-5b9c-72d8-384dc39e77fb " style=""><div id="fragment-94b5c223-f324-2c1a-a21d-b5c8ea6a968f"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-bb25fd23-2785-fe9b-7cb0-792f9a4443ec lfr-layout-structure-item-container " style=""><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-heading lfr-layout-structure-item-fb19754c-0c57-a359-cf5f-1b3ea45a40c7 " style=""><div id="fragment-b3c06bd6-9ad1-d9a5-cb1c-5eba762e6284"> <h3 class="component-heading mb-0 text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="text">Find your next dream job or find employees in controlling with Hays</h3></div><style>.fragment-heading-text-colored a {
	color: inherit;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-7d9733e2-5ce2-200d-1acd-f65b97b5a9d0 " style=""><div id="fragment-65895a6c-c58f-56b5-5a5e-5fa0fd9c6dcf"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-73e1e6fd-d1af-ab5b-fdfa-a67ad1be34f2 " style=""><div id="fragment-81f6d82f-5d2d-9f2a-88c9-5b858f13f7b2"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">When placing qualified controllers with your company, our recruiters use search networks and data analyses to create shortlists of our applicants. This allows us to access a large number of suitable candidates at any time, which we then place in accordance with your requirements.<br />
<br />
In order to best place you in a suitable vacancy in Controlling, we attach great importance to getting to know our applicants in the field of Controlling. This enables us to correctly assess your interests and priorities and place you in exciting job offers with suitable companies at any time.<br />
<br />
If the professional exchange and mutual interest between the applicant and the company are satisfactory, all relevant framework conditions are agreed with Hays. Applicants are then employed either directly by the company or by Hays via a temporary employment agency. Nothing stands in the way of a good working relationship!</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div></div></div> 
 </div>

<div id="hh-loader-omwo_" class="hh-item hh-item4">
    <div class="circle circle1"></div>
    <div class="circle circle2"></div>
    <div class="circle circle3"></div>

<script>
    if (window.location.protocol.indexOf('https') == 0){
        var el = document.createElement('meta')
        el.setAttribute('http-equiv', 'Content-Security-Policy')
        el.setAttribute('content', 'upgrade-insecure-requests')
        document.head.append(el)
    }
    var href = document.location.origin;
    href += "/en/jobsearch/job-offers"+ "/";
    href += 'p/1/';
    var s = "controller";
    s = s.replace(/\s/g, '+');
    console.log(s);
    href += '?q='+s+'&e=false';
    href += '&saveFilter=false';
    console.log("fetching from " + href);

    function loadJobLinks() {
        console.log("imloaded");
        var langAttributeValue = $('html').attr('lang');
        var buttonTitle;

        if(langAttributeValue === 'de-CH' || langAttributeValue === 'de-DE' ){
            buttonTitle = 'Jetzt ansehen';
        } else if (langAttributeValue === 'fr-FR') {
            buttonTitle = 'Regarder maintenant';
        }
        else if (langAttributeValue === 'en-GB') {
            buttonTitle = 'View now';
        }
        else {
            buttonTitle = 'Læs mere';
        }
        if ($(".search__result").length != 0){
            setTimeout(function() {
                $('.search__result').each(function(index){
                    var watchNowLink = $(this).find('.search__result__link').attr('href');
                    if($(this).find('.search__result__meta')){
                        $(this).append('<a class="h-job-profiles__related-jobs-links" href="'+watchNowLink+'">'+buttonTitle+'</a>');
                    }
                })
            }, 1000);}
    }

    function insert_jobs(){
        $("#publish-jobs-omwo_").load(href + ' .search__results .search__result:nth-child(-n+21)', function() {
            $('.search__result.text-center').remove();
            $('a.search__result__link').click (function(e){
                e.preventDefault();
                dataLayer.push(
                    {
                        'event': 'Link-Klick',
                        'eventkategorie': 'job-publisher-content-template',
                        'eventaktion': 'clicked' +$(this).attr("href")+ 'von:' + document.location.href,
                        'eventlabel': 'Klick auf einen Job'
                    }
                );
                console.log("datalayer is sent.");
                console.log($(this).attr("href"));
                var addressValue = $(this).attr("href");
                setTimeout(function () {
                    window.location.href = addressValue;
                }, 500);
            });

            setTimeout(function(){
                $("#publish-jobs-omwo_").slick({
                    /* variableWidth: true,*/
                    dots: true,
                    infinite: true,
                    slidesToShow:  3,
                    slidesToScroll: 1,
                    responsive: [
                        {
                            breakpoint: 900,
                            settings: {
                                slidesToShow: 2,
                                slidesToScroll: 1
                            }
                        },
                        {
                            breakpoint: 576,
                            settings: {
                                slidesToShow: 1,
                                slidesToScroll: 1,
                                centerMode:true,
                                centerPadding:'0'
                            }
                        }
                    ]
                });
                $(".lazy").slick({
                    lazyLoad: 'ondemand', // ondemand progressive anticipated
                    infinite: true
                });
            }, 100);

            loadJobLinks();


            $("#hh-loader-omwo_").hide();
            if ($('#publish-jobs-omwo_').is(':empty')) {
                console.log("No result");
                var h2Tag = document.createElement('H3');
                if ($('html').attr('lang') == "de-CH" || $('html').attr('lang') == "de-DE") {
                    h2Tag.innerHTML = "Für dieses Jobprofil wurden keine vakanten Stellen gefunden.";
                }
                if ($('html').attr('lang') == "fr-FR") {
                    h2Tag.innerHTML = "Aucun poste vacant trouvé pour ce profil.";
                }
                if ($('html').attr('lang') == "en-GB") {
                    h2Tag.innerHTML = "No job opportunities found for this profile.";
                }
                $('#publish-jobs-nojob-omwo_').prepend(h2Tag);
            }
        });
    }
    insert_jobs();
</script>

                </div>
            </div>
        <div class="fold-content  folded "><p>The controller (m/f/d) is responsible for the ongoing analysis and interpretation of company figures. This enables controllers to quickly recognize when a business, a specialist area or a product is developing differently than planned. In the event of an unfavorable company development, corrective measures can be taken in consultation with the management in order to put the company back on the road to success. At the beginning of a professional career as a controller (m/f/d), people join a company as junior controllers. Initially, junior controllers often have a supporting role and create budget plans, write analyses and reports and prepare data. With increasing professional experience, responsibility usually increases. The focus is then increasingly on strategy and management.</p></div>

	</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
(function() {var $ = AUI.$;var _ = AUI._;
	var onDestroyPortlet = function () {
		Liferay.detach('messagePosted', onMessagePosted);
		Liferay.detach('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);
	};

	Liferay.on('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);

	var onMessagePosted = function (event) {
		if (window.Analytics) {
			const eventProperties = {
				className: event.className,
				classPK: event.classPK,
				commentId: event.commentId,
				text: event.text,
			};

			const blogNode = document.querySelector(
				'[data-analytics-asset-id="' + event.classPK + '"]'
			);

			const dmNode = document.querySelector(
				'[data-analytics-file-entry-id="' + event.classPK + '"]'
			);

			if (blogNode) {
				eventProperties.title = blogNode.dataset.analyticsAssetTitle;
			}
			else if (dmNode) {
				eventProperties.title = dmNode.dataset.analyticsFileEntryTitle;
			}

			Analytics.send('posted', 'Comment', eventProperties);
		}
	};

	Liferay.on('messagePosted', onMessagePosted);
})();

	function getValueByAttribute(node, attr) {
		return (
			node.dataset[attr] ||
			(node.parentElement && node.parentElement.dataset[attr])
		);
	}

	function sendDocumentDownloadedAnalyticsEvent(anchor) {
		var fileEntryId = getValueByAttribute(
			anchor,
			'analyticsFileEntryId'
		);
		var title = getValueByAttribute(
			anchor,
			'analyticsFileEntryTitle'
		);
		var version = getValueByAttribute(
			anchor,
			'analyticsFileEntryVersion'
		);

		if (fileEntryId) {
			Analytics.send('documentDownloaded', 'Document', {
				groupId: themeDisplay.getScopeGroupId(),
				fileEntryId,
				preview: !!window._com_liferay_document_library_analytics_isViewFileEntry,
				title,
				version,
			});
		}
	}

	function handleDownloadClick(event) {
		if (window.Analytics) {
			if (event.target.nodeName.toLowerCase() === 'a') {
				sendDocumentDownloadedAnalyticsEvent(
					event.target
				);
			}
			else if (
				event.target.parentNode &&
				event.target.parentNode.nodeName.toLowerCase() === 'a'
			) {
				sendDocumentDownloadedAnalyticsEvent(
					event.target.parentNode
				);
			}
			else {
				var target = event.target;
				var matchTextContent =
					target.textContent &&
					target.textContent.toLowerCase() ===
						'download';
				var matchTitle =
					target.title && target.title.toLowerCase() === 'download';
				var matchAction = target.action === 'download';
				var matchLexiconIcon = !!target.querySelector(
					'.lexicon-icon-download'
				);
				var matchLexiconClassName = target.classList.contains(
					'lexicon-icon-download'
				);
				var matchParentTitle =
					target.parentNode &&
					target.parentNode.title &&
					target.parentNode.title.toLowerCase() === 'download';
				var matchParentLexiconClassName =
					target.parentNode &&
					target.parentNode.classList.contains('lexicon-icon-download');

				if (
					matchTextContent ||
					matchTitle ||
					matchParentTitle ||
					matchAction ||
					matchLexiconIcon ||
					matchLexiconClassName ||
					matchParentLexiconClassName
				) {
					var selectedFiles = document.querySelectorAll(
						'.form .custom-control-input:checked'
					);

					selectedFiles.forEach(({value}) => {
						var selectedFile = document.querySelector(
							'[data-analytics-file-entry-id="' + value + '"]'
						);

						sendDocumentDownloadedAnalyticsEvent(
							selectedFile
						);
					});
				}
			}
		}
	}

	Liferay.once('destroyPortlet', () => {
		document.body.removeEventListener(
			'click',
			handleDownloadClick
		);
	});

	Liferay.once('portletReady', () => {
		document.body.addEventListener(
			'click',
			handleDownloadClick
		);
	});

(function() {var $ = AUI.$;var _ = AUI._;
	var onVote = function (event) {
		if (window.Analytics) {
			let title = event.contentTitle;

			if (!title) {
				const dmNode = document.querySelector(
					'[data-analytics-file-entry-id="' + event.classPK + '"]'
				);

				if (dmNode) {
					title = dmNode.dataset.analyticsFileEntryTitle;
				}
			}

			Analytics.send('VOTE', 'Ratings', {
				className: event.className,
				classPK: event.classPK,
				ratingType: event.ratingType,
				score: event.score,
				title,
			});
		}
	};

	var onDestroyPortlet = function () {
		Liferay.detach('ratings:vote', onVote);
		Liferay.detach('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);
	};

	Liferay.on('ratings:vote', onVote);
	Liferay.on('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);
})();
(function() {var $ = AUI.$;var _ = AUI._;
	var onShare = function (data) {
		if (window.Analytics) {
			Analytics.send('shared', 'SocialBookmarks', {
				className: data.className,
				classPK: data.classPK,
				type: data.type,
				url: data.url,
			});
		}
	};

	var onDestroyPortlet = function () {
		Liferay.detach('socialBookmarks:share', onShare);
		Liferay.detach('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);
	};

	Liferay.on('socialBookmarks:share', onShare);
	Liferay.on('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);
})();

	if (window.svg4everybody && Liferay.Data.ICONS_INLINE_SVG) {
		svg4everybody(
			{
				polyfill: true,
				validate: function (src, svg, use) {
					return !src || !src.startsWith('#');
				}
			}
		);
	}

(function() {var $ = AUI.$;var _ = AUI._;
	Liferay.Util.delegate(
		document,
		'focusin',
		'.portlet',
		function(event) {
			event.delegateTarget.closest('.portlet').classList.add('open');
		}
	);

	Liferay.Util.delegate(
		document,
		'focusout',
		'.portlet',
		function(event) {
			event.delegateTarget.closest('.portlet').classList.remove('open');
		}
	);
})();

	// <![CDATA[

		

		Liferay.currentURL = '\x2fen\x2fjob-profiles\x2fcontroller';
		Liferay.currentURLEncoded = '\x252Fen\x252Fjob-profiles\x252Fcontroller';

	// ]]>


		// <![CDATA[
			
				function loadMoinScript(url, id, callback) {
  var script = document.createElement("script");
  script.type = "text/javascript";
  if (script.readyState) {
    script.onreadystatechange = function () {
      if (script.readyState == "loaded" || script.readyState == "complete") {
        script.onreadystatechange = null;
        callback();
      }
    };
  } else {
    script.readyState = function () {
      callback();
    };
  }
  script.src = url;
  if (id) {
    script.id = id;
  }
  document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
}
window.addEventListener("load", function () {
  if (typeof truste !== "undefined") {
    const TRUST_FUNCTIONAL = 2;
    let result = truste.cma.callApi("getConsentDecision", window.location.host);
    if (
      result.consentDecision >= TRUST_FUNCTIONAL &&
      !window.location.href.includes("/lp/")
    ) {
      if (document.documentElement.lang == "de-DE") {
        loadMoinScript(
          "https://widget.moin.ai/moin-loader.js?id=ee05741e33c129f2532ec938462da9a13e2a95e725ffb8049cbf789431fc028c&channelid=ee05741e33c129f2532ec938462da9a13e2a95e725ffb8049cbf789431fc028c&v=" +
          Date.now(),
          "moinloader"
        );
      } else if (document.documentElement.lang == "en-GB") {
        loadMoinScript(
          "https://widget.moin.ai/moin-loader.js?id=ee05741e33c129f2532ec938462da9a13e2a95e725ffb8049cbf789431fc028c&channelid=ee05741e33c129f2532ec938462da9a13e2a95e725ffb8049cbf789431fc028c-en&v=" +
          Date.now(),
          "moinloader"
        );
      }

      loadMoinScript(
        "https://widget.moin.ai/zendesk-web-sdk.js?v=" + Date.now(),
        ""
      );
    }
  }
});



window.chatWidgetReady = function () {
  window.knowhere.api.setWidgetzIndex(50);
  window.knowhere.api.setWidgetPosition(0, 70, "px", true);
  $("#moin-ai-widget").css({ maxHeight: "95vh" });
  //  window.knowhere.api.hideWidget();
  let moin_message = null;
  const isMobile = /iPhone|iPad|iPod|Android/i.test(navigator.userAgent);

  window.knowhere.api.on('widget.interaction', function (data) {
    moin_message = data;
    console.log('WIDGET HANDLER', JSON.stringify(moin_message));

    //console.log(' WIDGET HANDLER', JSON.stringify(data.message.action),JSON.stringify(data.message.source));
    dataLayer.push({ 'event': 'moin-ai-chat', 'eventkategorie': 'moin_ai', 'eventaktion': 'widget-interaction', 'eventlabel': "current.page: " + window.location.href + " is.mobile " + isMobile + " data.message.action:" + JSON.stringify(data.message.action) + ", data.message.message:" + JSON.stringify(data.message.source) });
  })

  window.knowhere.api.on('user.click', function (data) {
    moin_message = data;
   // console.log('CLICK HANDLER', JSON.stringify(moin_message));

    //console.log(' CLICK HANDLER', JSON.stringify(data.message.source),JSON.stringify(data.message.text),JSON.stringify(data.message.target));
    dataLayer.push({ 'event': 'moin-ai-chat', 'eventkategorie': 'moin_ai', 'eventaktion': 'user-click', 'eventlabel': "current.page: " + window.location.href + " is.mobile " + isMobile + " data.message.source:" + JSON.stringify(data.message.source) + ", data.message.text:" + JSON.stringify(data.message.text) + ", data.message.target:" + JSON.stringify(data.message.target) });
  })

  window.knowhere.api.on('user.input', function (data) {
    moin_message = data;
    //console.log('USER HANDLER', JSON.stringify(moin_message));

    //console.log(' USER HANDLER', JSON.stringify(data.message.action),JSON.stringify(data.message.message));
    dataLayer.push({ 'event': 'moin-ai-chat', 'eventkategorie': 'moin_ai', 'eventaktion': 'user-input', 'eventlabel': "current.page: " + window.location.href + " is.mobile " + isMobile + " data.message.action:" + JSON.stringify(data.message.action)});
  })
};


//Haysworld navi tracking dont remove
$(".hw-custom-navi a").each(function () {
  $(this).attr(
    "onclick",
    "dataLayer.push({'event': 'Think Ahead','eventkategorie': 'Navigationspunkt','eventaktion': 'menu-name: '+ this.innerText,'eventlabel':$(this).attr('href')});"
  );
});

//Haysworld buttons track

$(".h-btn-track-extern").each(function () {
  $(this).attr(
    "onclick",
    "dataLayer.push({'event': 'Button', 'eventkategorie': 'externer Link', 'eventaktion': window.location.href, 'eventlabel': $(this).attr('href')});"
  );
});

$("a").each(function () {
  if ($(this).attr("href") && !$(this).attr("onclick")) {
    var hrefValue = $(this).attr('href');
    var eventKategorie = hrefValue.includes(".hays.") || hrefValue.startsWith("/") ? "interner Link" : "externer Link";
    var currentLocation = window.location.pathname;
    var eventType = $(this).hasClass("hays-btn") || $(this).hasClass("h-btn") ? "Button" : "Link-Klick";
    var eventLabel = hrefValue;

    // Remove "https://www." or "https://" if it's an external link
    if (eventKategorie === "externer Link") {
      if (eventLabel.startsWith("https://www.")) {
        eventLabel = eventLabel.replace("https://www.", "");
      } else if (eventLabel.startsWith("https://")) {
        eventLabel = eventLabel.replace("https://", "");
      }
    }

    $(this).attr(
      "onclick",
      "dataLayer.push({'event': '" + eventType + "', 'eventkategorie': '" + eventKategorie + "', 'eventaktion': 'von: " + currentLocation + "', 'eventlabel': 'nach: " + eventLabel + "'});"
    );
  }
});

            $(".popup__menu").addClass("hidden");
            $(".button_back_to_mobile_level").removeClass("hidden");
            $(".row.border_bottom_mobile_menu").addClass("hidden");
            $(".mobile-navitem-title").addClass("hidden");
            $(".row.button_back_to_mobile_menu").removeClass("hidden");
            $(".mobile-navitem-title.collapse_my_hays_mobile_menu").removeClass("hidden");
            $(".popup__menu.collapse_my_hays_mobile_menu").removeClass("hidden");
        } else if (mobileLayoutStory != "" && $(".mobile_layout_"+mobileLayoutStory).length > 1) {
            $(".row.border_bottom_mobile_menu").addClass("hidden");

            $("span.button_back_to_mobile_menu").removeClass("hidden");
            $(".button_back_to_mobile_level").removeClass("hidden");

            $(".mobile-navitem-title").addClass("hidden");
            $(".mobile_layout_"+mobileLayoutStory).removeClass("hidden");

        $("#navigation-container").children().each(function(item) {
            if ($(this).find(".top-navigation-flyout").length != 0) {
                $(this).mouseenter(function() {
                    $("#body-shadow").addClass("body-shadow-show");
                }).mouseleave(function() {
                    $("#body-shadow").removeClass("body-shadow-show");
                    navigationHistory(layoutStory);
                });
            }
       });

        $(".nav-list__item").mouseenter(function() {
            let count = $(this).children().find("ul:lt(1)").children().length;
            if ($(this).children(".container-grid:lt(1)").hasClass("container-grid-third") || $(this).parent().children().length > count && count != 0 && !$(this).find(".nav-list:lt(1)").hasClass("scrollbar-nav-items")) {
                $(this).children(".container-grid:lt(1)").addClass("compare-children-height");
                $(this).find(".nav-list:lt(1)").addClass("compare-children-height-ul");
            }
        }).mouseleave(function() {
            $(this).children(".container-grid:lt(1)").removeClass("compare-children-height");
            $(this).find(".nav-list:lt(1)").removeClass("compare-children-height-ul");
        });

        });

                <script>
                    setCookie("hays_rdrt", window.location.pathname + window.location.search);
                    const utmString = getUtmPartOfString(window.location.pathname + window.location.search);


                    function setCookie(name, value) {
                        const date = new Date();
                        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (1*24*60*60*1000));
                        let expires = "expires="+ date.toUTCString();
                        document.cookie = name + "=" + value + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
                    }

                    function setUTMCookie(name, value) {
                        const date = new Date();
                        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (15*60*1000));
                        let expires = "expires="+ date.toUTCString();
                        document.cookie = name + "=" + value + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
                    }

                    function getCookie(name){
                        const cookies = document.cookie.split(';');
                        for (let i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++){
                            const cookie = cookies[i].trim();
                            if(cookie.startsWith(name + '=')){
                                return cookie.substring(name.length + 1);
                            }
                        }
                        return null;
                    }

                    function getUtmPartOfString(url){
                        const utmParams = extractAndCheckUtm(url);
                        const utmParamsUrl = window.location.pathname;
                        if(utmParams){
                            let modiefiedUtm = utmParams.replace(/=/g, "/");
                            setUTMCookie('utm_params',encodeURIComponent(modiefiedUtm));
                            setUTMCookie('utm_params_initial',utmParamsUrl);
                            return modiefiedUtm;
                        }else {
                            const storedQuery = getCookie('utm_params');
                            if(storedQuery && storedQuery.includes("utm")){
                                return storedQuery;
                            }
                        }
                        return null;
                    }

                    function extractAndCheckUtm(url){
                        const utmStringIndex = url.indexOf("?");
                        if(utmStringIndex !== -1){
                            const extractUtm = url.substring(utmStringIndex + 1)
                            return extractUtm.includes("utm") ? extractUtm : null;
                        }
                        return null;
                    }
                </script>

                <script>
                    var input = document.getElementById("what");
                    input.addEventListener("keypress", function(event) {
                        if (event.key === "Enter") {
                            event.preventDefault();
                            document.getElementById("searchbar-trigger-btn").click();
                        }
                    });
                </script>
